# Meta data

<pre>
Ramon benchmark for Z3
-
Job description: aproximate sort by degree
Job tag: skinny_deg
Runner: rise-runner-2
Z3 repo: Z3Prover/z3
Z3 commit: c39a0ba12d000bd765622f25ca0e7cffe0f5b237
Z3 branch: skinny_deg
Z3 options: "-T:60"
Z3 inputs: inputs/QF_NIA_small
Z3 commit message: nra: estimate degree (not size) of inlined constraint polynomial

In nra_solver, replace constraint_expansion_size (which approximated
total monic size and treated terms as opaque leaves) with
constraint_expansion_degree.

The new estimate upper-bounds the degree of the constraint polynomial
in its highest leaf variable after fully inlining all monics and
terms. For each constraint we:

  1. pick the leaf variable x with the largest LP index reachable
     from the constraint (matches the nlsat variable order: leaves
     are created in ascending LP-index order in check_assignment,
     so the largest-index leaf is the highest-ordered nlsat var);
  2. recursively compute deg_x(v) for each top-level v in the
     constraint via var_degree_in:
       leaf  : 1 if v == x else 0
       monic : sum of factor degrees (deg of product)
       term  : max of summand degrees (upper bound for deg of sum;
               cancellation between summands can only lower it);
  3. return max_i deg_x(v_i) over the constraint's coeff*v_i terms,
     which upper-bounds deg_x(sum_i c_i * v_i).

The recursion is acyclic (factors are introduced before composites)
and each variable is memoized per call.

The caller in check_assignment is updated to use the renamed
function and cache (expansion_degree_cache); the sort and heuristic
are otherwise unchanged.

Co-authored-by: Copilot <223556219+Copilot@users.noreply.github.com>

</pre>
